CornImages = CornImage.objects.all()
index = 0
for corn_image in CornImages:
    related_actualBox = actualBoxess[index]
    BoxImage.objects.bulk_create(related_actualBox)

    related_actualBox = BoxImage.objects.all()

    for actual_box in related_actualBox:
        corn_image.actualBoxes.add(actual_box)
    index += 1
